One of the rooms I booked didn‚Äôt get cleaned in time for our check in and we were able to change rooms the following morning with no additional charges.

Overall quality of the hotel is good, hotel breakfast is the best option considering food options nearby are nearly 1km away (******* takeaway is possible too).
On the morning of checkout, we checked out prior to breakfast being served and the hotel were kind enough to provide us takeaway breakfast to replace our breakfast tickets for the morning.

Overall 4.5/5

In Beijing at the end of March, the breath of spring is already very strong. Yellow jasmine flowers and green willow buds dot every corner of the city. The last time I came to Beijing was early winter. More than three months had passed in the blink of an eye, and my mood was completely different. It just so happens that the hotel's new renovation has been completed not long ago. There is no trace of 30 years ago. It is like a brand new hotel. The check-in procedure is very fast. The entrance of the hotel lobby is 20 meters away from the Dongsi****iao Bridge subway station. How convenient is it? The most important thing is that when other hotels are following the market and prices are generally rising, only the Swissotel is relatively righteous, and the price is almost the same as usual. It's less than 1,000 yuan including breakfast for two, which is really a great price in this area.

The overall service of the hotel is very good. After communicating by phone, you can check in a little earlier and check out two hours later, which is very humane. The weather in Beijing has been awkward recently. It's hot, it's really hot, it can reach 27¬∞ at noon, and it's cold. I just returned to the hotel at night and it was still quite cold with the wind from the hotel's central air conditioner. After we called the front desk, they took the initiative to send us a heater. The response speed was beyond imagination.
What I want to praise the most is the breakfast here. It is really great. It can be said that it is the best breakfast among all the five-star hotels I have stayed in. Of course, I am also sorry for my ignorance. I have stayed in fewer five-star hotels, but in my opinion, the breakfast of Swissotel is really first-class and impeccable! A combination of Chinese and Western, children and the elderly like it, I can't help but praise it!

To be honest, the room facilities are incomparable to the latest five-star hotels, but the service and other software are very good. The bathroom is separated into dry and wet areas, and the space is not large. Disposable toiletries do not need to be specifically requested, they have been placed in the bathroom, and they are truly super environmentally friendly! The toothbrush has a wooden handle, and the bag for toothpaste is a paper bag instead of a plastic bag. The amount is also very accurate, which is the amount of two meals, so there will be no waste.

Later, we went to the gym and swimming pool on the 3rd floor to take a look. Like the swimming pool! Although it is not big, the light is super good. Even on a short holiday, there are not many people and the environment is very good!

Recommend Swissotel! The king of comprehensive cost performance!

Maybe none of them will be touched, but the Coke in the Swiss Hotel refrigerator starts at 28 yuan, and if you are used to other hotels, you will still have to pay if you are not careful.
2. Here comes the important point. Before turning on the shower in the bathroom, you have to listen to the whistle of the shower for one to two minutes before you can take a normal bath. Moreover, the shower is old and the water output is not very large.
3. Normally, bathroom non-slip mats are placed in a conspicuous place in the bathroom to prevent guests from slipping when they cannot find them while taking a bath. I called to inquire about the location and found out that they were placed in a hidden place under the sink outside the bathroom. They are the same color as the hair dryer bag. , you may not be able to detect it even if your eyesight is not good.
4. Normally, hotel bathrobes are hung in the closet. Guests can find them when they open the closet after taking a shower. They are placed on the partition above the closet. If a woman is not taller than 1.7 meters, she will look up and look for them. I really can‚Äôt find the experience of staying in a hotel before.
5. You have to ask to know how to use the air conditioner, and you still have to call again to help turn it on when you come back.
The overall experience of staying in the hotel is very inhumane. It is estimated that the management basically does not like the fireworks of the world. For people like us who need to do our own daily life, the experience of staying in other luxury or well-known high-end hotels is actually better.
